      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 7th century
       </b>
       . During the period 601 to 700 there were 251
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 90 were partial, 90 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 67 were total, and 4 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was five, in 604 and 669, and two months, April 618 and March 629, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>
